\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filter__design_8py_source_l03669}03669\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ type\ ==\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{'butter'}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filter__design_8py_source_l03670}03670\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ GSTOP\ =\ 10\ **\ (0.1\ *\ abs(gstop))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filter__design_8py_source_l03671}03671\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ GPASS\ =\ 10\ **\ (0.1\ *\ abs(gpass))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filter__design_8py_source_l03672}03672\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ n\ =\ (log10((GSTOP\ -\/\ 1.0)\ /\ (GPASS\ -\/\ 1.0))\ /\ (2\ *\ log10(nat)))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filter__design_8py_source_l03673}03673\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{elif}\ type\ ==\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{'cheby'}:}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filter__design_8py_source_l03676}03676\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ n\ =\ arccosh(sqrt((GSTOP\ -\/\ 1.0)\ /\ (GPASS\ -\/\ 1.0)))\ /\ arccosh(nat)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filter__design_8py_source_l03677}03677\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{elif}\ type\ ==\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{'ellip'}:}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filter__design_8py_source_l03679}03679\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ GPASS\ =\ 10\ **\ (0.1\ *\ gpass)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filter__design_8py_source_l03680}03680\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ arg1\ =\ sqrt((GPASS\ -\/\ 1.0)\ /\ (GSTOP\ -\/\ 1.0))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filter__design_8py_source_l03681}03681\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ arg0\ =\ 1.0\ /\ nat}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filter__design_8py_source_l03682}03682\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ d0\ =\ special.ellipk([arg0\ **\ 2,\ 1\ -\/\ arg0\ **\ 2])}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filter__design_8py_source_l03683}03683\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ d1\ =\ special.ellipk([arg1\ **\ 2,\ 1\ -\/\ arg1\ **\ 2])}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filter__design_8py_source_l03684}03684\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ n\ =\ (d0[0]\ *\ d1[1]\ /\ (d0[1]\ *\ d1[0]))}
